txtPostIPANbr

XP_YLine_Translation,             ProjectID = varCurrentProjectID,             NDB_Yline_IPA         )     ) && 
StartsWith(         LookUp(             CS_EXP_YLine_Translation,             ProjectID = varCurrentProjectID,

varCurrentProjectID,         NDB_Yline_IPA     ) )  "Text input"
